\doxysubsection{详细描述}
The Fast\+Flow abstract contanier for a parallel activity (actor). 

Implements {\ttfamily \doxylink{classff_1_1ff__node}{ff\+\_\+node}}, i.\+e. the general container for a parallel activity. From the orchestration viewpoint, the process model to be employed is a CSP/\+Actor hybrid model where activities ({\ttfamily ff\+\_\+nodes}) are named and the data paths between processes are clearly identified. {\ttfamily ff\+\_\+nodes} synchronise each another via abstract units of SPSC communications and synchronisation (namely 1\+:1 channels), which models data dependency between two {\ttfamily ff\+\_\+nodes}. It is used to encapsulate sequential portions of code implementing functions.

{\ttfamily In} a multicore, a \doxylink{classff_1_1ff__node}{ff\+\_\+node} is implemented as non-\/blocking thread. It is not and should not be confused with a task. Typically a {\ttfamily \doxylink{classff_1_1ff__node}{ff\+\_\+node}} uses the 100\% of one CPU context (i.\+e. one core, either physical or HT, if any). Overall, the number of ff\+\_\+nodes running should not exceed the number of logical cores of the platform.

{\ttfamily \doxylink{bench__gemm_8cpp_addc86e8508f14411ec98f521c520f875}{A}} \doxylink{classff_1_1ff__node}{ff\+\_\+node} behaves as a loop that gets an input (i.\+e. the parameter of {\ttfamily svc} method) and produces one or more outputs (i.\+e. return parameter of {\ttfamily svc} method or parameter of the {\ttfamily ff\+\_\+send\+\_\+out} method that can be called in the {\ttfamily svc} method). The loop complete on the output of the special value "{}end-\/of\+\_\+stream"{} (EOS). The EOS is propagated across channels to the next {\ttfamily \doxylink{classff_1_1ff__node}{ff\+\_\+node}}. ~\newline


Key methods are\+: {\ttfamily svc\+\_\+init}, {\ttfamily svc\+\_\+end} (optional), and {\ttfamily svc} (pure virtual, mandatory). The {\ttfamily svc\+\_\+init} method is called once at node initialization, while the {\ttfamily svn\+\_\+end} method is called after a EOS task has been returned.

This class is defined in \doxylink{node_8hpp}{node.\+hpp}

virtual \mbox{\hyperlink{ittnotify__static_8h_a61af67d9d838a9497ca5b188dabc1aa0}{void}} ff\+::ff\+\_\+node\+::eosnotify (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{eabase_8h_a831c6b6852c6d34448e30a88c34539fd}{ssize\+\_\+t}}}]{}{ = {\ttfamily -\/1}}\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [inline]}, {\ttfamily [virtual]}}



EOS callback 

This method is called when an EOS has just been received from one input channel. Inside this method it is possible to call ff\+\_\+send\+\_\+out to produce data elements in output (this is not possible in the svc\+\_\+end method). The parameter
\begin{DoxyParams}{参数}
{\em id} & is the ID of the channel that received the EOS. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}

\Hypertarget{classff_1_1ff__node_a66ddc4b89e7a2fd1b8d4a02c94eb9408}\index{ff::ff\_node@{ff::ff\_node}!ff\_send\_out@{ff\_send\_out}}

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{ff\_send\_out()}{ff\_send\_out()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{classff_1_1ff__node_a66ddc4b89e7a2fd1b8d4a02c94eb9408} 
virtual \mbox{\hyperlink{sugar_8h_abb452686968e48b67397da5f97445f5b}{bool}} ff\+::ff\+\_\+node\+::ff\+\_\+send\+\_\+out (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{ittnotify__static_8h_a61af67d9d838a9497ca5b188dabc1aa0}{void}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{task}{, }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{sugar_8h_ae4f82344f573c70aa1066a2394bba345}{int}}}]{id}{ = {\ttfamily -\/1}, }\item[{unsigned long}]{retry}{ = {\ttfamily ((unsigned~long)-\/1)}, }\item[{unsigned long}]{ticks}{ = {\ttfamily (\mbox{\hyperlink{classff_1_1ff__node_a66bb1559f1f0863a0034633e82795b0ca2824e434c3e717a7df8664d8af4b62cc}{TICKS2\+WAIT}})}}\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [inline]}, {\ttfamily [virtual]}}



Sends out the task 

It allows to emit tasks on output stream without returning from the {\ttfamily svc} method. Make the \doxylink{classff_1_1ff__node}{ff\+\_\+node} to emit zero or more tasks per input task


\begin{DoxyParams}{参数}
{\em task} & a pointer to the task \\
\hline
{\em retry} & number of tries to put (nonbloking partial) the task to output channel \\
\hline
{\em ticks} & delay between successive retries \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}

Nonblocking put into the input channel 

Wait-\/free and fence-\/free (under TSO) This is called by a different node (e.\+g., lb) to push data into the node\textquotesingle{}s input queue.

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{skipfirstpop()}{skipfirstpop()}\hspace{0.1cm}{\footnotesize\ttfamily [1/2]}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{classff_1_1ff__node_a71789627f48cb9f466c50601a881c7bc} 
\mbox{\hyperlink{sugar_8h_abb452686968e48b67397da5f97445f5b}{bool}} ff\+::ff\+\_\+node\+::skipfirstpop (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}{}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption}) const\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [inline]}, {\ttfamily [protected]}}



Gets the status of spontaneous start 

If {\ttfamily true} the {\ttfamily \doxylink{classff_1_1ff__node}{ff\+\_\+node}} execute the {\ttfamily svc} method spontaneusly before receiving a task on the input channel. {\ttfamily skipfirstpop} makes it possible to define a "{}producer"{} node that produce the stream.

\begin{DoxyReturn}{返回}
{\ttfamily true} if skip-\/the-\/first-\/element mode is set, {\ttfamily false} otherwise
\end{DoxyReturn}
Example\+: l1\+\_\+ff\+\_\+nodes\+\_\+graph.\+cpp \Hypertarget{classff_1_1ff__node_a949d963e759f57c978bd0d85f89ed1b3}\index{ff::ff\_node@{ff::ff\_node}!skipfirstpop@{skipfirstpop}}
\index{skipfirstpop@{skipfirstpop}!ff::ff\_node@{ff::ff\_node}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{skipfirstpop()}{skipfirstpop()}\hspace{0.1cm}{\footnotesize\ttfamily [2/2]}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{classff_1_1ff__node_a949d963e759f57c978bd0d85f89ed1b3} 
virtual \mbox{\hyperlink{ittnotify__static_8h_a61af67d9d838a9497ca5b188dabc1aa0}{void}} ff\+::ff\+\_\+node\+::skipfirstpop (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{sugar_8h_abb452686968e48b67397da5f97445f5b}{bool}}}]{sk}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [inline]}, {\ttfamily [protected]}, {\ttfamily [virtual]}}



Set the \doxylink{classff_1_1ff__node}{ff\+\_\+node} to start with no input task 

Setting it to true let the {\ttfamily \doxylink{classff_1_1ff__node}{ff\+\_\+node}} execute the {\ttfamily svc} method spontaneusly before receiving a task on the input channel. {\ttfamily skipfirstpop} makes it possible to define a "{}producer"{} node that starts the network.


\begin{DoxyParams}{参数}
{\em sk} & {\ttfamily true} start spontaneously (\texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}task will be NULL) \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}

virtual \mbox{\hyperlink{sugar_8h_ae4f82344f573c70aa1066a2394bba345}{int}} ff\+::ff\+\_\+node\+::svc\+\_\+init (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}{}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [inline]}, {\ttfamily [virtual]}}



Service initialisation 

Called after run-\/time initialisation (e.\+g. thread spawning) but before to start to get items from input stream (can be useful for initialisation of parallel activities, e.\+g. manual thread pinning that cannot be done in the costructor because threads stil do not exist).

\begin{DoxyReturn}{返回}
0 
\end{DoxyReturn}
